          <h2 class="headers__H2-kmc2rk-1 hulPZj">
           What is Postman?
          </h2>
          <p class="headers__Paragraph-kmc2rk-5 jkXoBo">
           Postman is a collaboration platform for API development. Postman's features simplify each step of building an API and streamline collaboration so you can create better APIs—faster.
          </p>
         </div>
         <div class="col-12 col-lg-4 d-flex align-items-stretch mt-4">
          <div class="card__CardContainer-sc-1czcsjw-0 iCeEMd">

            API Client
           </h3>
           <p class="headers__Paragraph-kmc2rk-5 dcnZyk">
            Quickly and easily send REST, SOAP, and GraphQL requests directly within Postman.
           </p>
           <div class="card__CardLinkContainer-sc-1czcsjw-1 iMPqx">
            <a class="styles__PostmanLink-wn1fs2-0 deAgYN" href="/product/api-client/">

            </a>
           </div>

            Automated Testing
           </h3>
           <p class="headers__Paragraph-kmc2rk-5 dcnZyk">

      <section class="Describe__Section-sc-1np55hj-0 gYSvod">
       <div class="container">
        <div class="row">
         <h2 class="headers__H2-kmc2rk-1 hulPZj col-12 text-center mb-5">
          Why Postman?
         </h2>
        </div>
        <div class="row justify-content-center">
         <div class="col-sm-12 col-md-6 col-lg-3 mb-3 mb-md-4 mb-lg-2">
          <div class="Describe__CardStyle-sc-1np55hj-1 jhWNlQ h-100">
           <h3 class="headers__H3-kmc2rk-2 fwpKHr text-center h4">
            It's Free and Easy to Start
           </h3>
           <div class="Describe__CardContent-sc-1np55hj-2 llhzag text-center">
            <p>
             Just
             <a href="https://identity.getpostman.com/signup?continue=https%3A%2F%2Fgo.postman.co%2Fbuild" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
              sign up for the Postman App
             </a>
             and send your first request in minutes. Postman is free to download and use for teams of any size.
            </p>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="col-sm-12 col-md-6 col-lg-3 mb-3 mb-md-4 mb-lg-2">
          <div class="Describe__CardStyle-sc-1np55hj-1 jhWNlQ h-100">
           <h3 class="headers__H3-kmc2rk-2 fwpKHr text-center h4">
            Wide support for all APIs and Schemas
           </h3>
           <div class="Describe__CardContent-sc-1np55hj-2 llhzag text-center">
            <p>
             Make any kind of API call—REST, SOAP, or plain HTTP—and easily inspect even the largest responses. Postman also has built—in support for popular data formats such as OpenAPI GraphQL, and RAML.
            </p>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="col-sm-12 col-md-6 col-lg-3 mb-3 mb-md-4 mb-lg-2">
          <div class="Describe__CardStyle-sc-1np55hj-1 jhWNlQ h-100">
           <h3 class="headers__H3-kmc2rk-2 fwpKHr text-center h4">
            It's Extensible
           </h3>
           <div class="Describe__CardContent-sc-1np55hj-2 llhzag text-center">
            <p>
             Customize Postman for your needs with the Postman API. Integrate test suites into your preferred CI/CD service with
             <a href="https://learning.postman.com/docs/postman/collection-runs/command-line-integration-with-newman/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">
              Newman
             </a>
             , our command line collection runner.
            </p>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="col-sm-12 col-md-6 col-lg-3 mb-3 mb-md-4 mb-lg-2">
          <div class="Describe__CardStyle-sc-1np55hj-1 jhWNlQ h-100">
           <h3 class="headers__H3-kmc2rk-2 fwpKHr text-center h4">
            Support and Community
           </h3>
           <div class="Describe__CardContent-sc-1np55hj-2 llhzag text-center">
            <p>
             We continually make improvements and add new features based on feedback from our community of over 13 million users—who can also help you get the most out of Postman on our
             <a href="https://community.postman.com/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">
              community forum
             </a>
             .
            </p>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
      </section>
     </div>
